<script>function JwplayerWrapper2() {
  var self = this;
  var playerInstance;
  var adEl;
  var adMediaContainerEl;
  var playerHeight;
  var playerOffsetTop;
  var isScrollTimeout;
  var isClosed = false;
  self.jwhavejwplayerlib = function() {
    if (typeof (jwplayer) != "undefined" && jwplayer != null && typeof (jwplayer.defaults.advertising) != "undefined" && jwplayer.defaults.advertising != null) return true;
    return false;
  };
  self.jwhavedefaultadtag = function() {
    if (typeof (jwplayer.defaults.advertising.tag) != "undefined" && jwplayer.defaults.advertising.tag != null) return true;
    return false;
  };
  self.jwhavescheduleadtag = function() {
    if (typeof (jwplayer.defaults.advertising.schedule) != "undefined" && jwplayer.defaults.advertising.schedule != null) return true;
    return false;
  };
  self.jwhaveadditionaladtargets = function() {
return true;
  };
  self.jwappenddefaultadtagwithadditional = function() {
    if (self.jwhaveadditionaladtargets() && self.jwhavedefaultadtag()) {
      if (jwplayer.defaults.advertising.tag.indexOf("cust_params=") > 0) {
        jwplayer.defaults.advertising.tag = jwplayer.defaults.advertising.tag.replace("cust_params=", "cust_params=make%3Dany%26model%3Dany%26city%3Dhalifax%26year%3Dany%26condition%3Dnew%2Cused%2Ccpo%26fuel_type%3Dany%26siteenvironment%3Dwww%2Ctest%26variation%3Dnone%2Cnone%7Cnone%26province%3Dnova_scotia%26buying_options%3Dany%26category%3Dcars_trucks_suvs%26price%3Dnan_nan".concat("%3D"));
      } else {
        jwplayer.defaults.advertising.tag = jwplayer.defaults.advertising.tag.concat(" & ", "cust_params=make%3Dany%26model%3Dany%26city%3Dhalifax%26year%3Dany%26condition%3Dnew%2Cused%2Ccpo%26fuel_type%3Dany%26siteenvironment%3Dwww%2Ctest%26variation%3Dnone%2Cnone%7Cnone%26province%3Dnova_scotia%26buying_options%3Dany%26category%3Dcars_trucks_suvs%26price%3Dnan_nan");
      }
    }
  };
  self.jwappendscheduleadtagwithadditional = function() {
    if (!window.custParamsInjected && self.jwhaveadditionaladtargets() && self.jwhavescheduleadtag()) {
      $.each(jwplayer.defaults.advertising.schedule, function(index, value) {
        window.custParamsInjected = true;
        if (value.tag.indexOf("cust_params=") > 0) {
          value.tag = value.tag.replace("cust_params=", "cust_params=make%3Dany%26model%3Dany%26city%3Dhalifax%26year%3Dany%26condition%3Dnew%2Cused%2Ccpo%26fuel_type%3Dany%26siteenvironment%3Dwww%2Ctest%26variation%3Dnone%2Cnone%7Cnone%26province%3Dnova_scotia%26buying_options%3Dany%26category%3Dcars_trucks_suvs%26price%3Dnan_nan".concat("%3D"));
        } else {
          value.tag = value.tag.concat("&", "cust_params=make%3Dany%26model%3Dany%26city%3Dhalifax%26year%3Dany%26condition%3Dnew%2Cused%2Ccpo%26fuel_type%3Dany%26siteenvironment%3Dwww%2Ctest%26variation%3Dnone%2Cnone%7Cnone%26province%3Dnova_scotia%26buying_options%3Dany%26category%3Dcars_trucks_suvs%26price%3Dnan_nan");
        }
      });
    }
  };
  // math functions related to scroll and offset positions relative to player
  self.getScrollTop = function() {
    var documentEl = document.documentElement;
    return (window.pageYOffset || documentEl.scrollTop) - (documentEl.clientTop || 0);
  };
  self.getElementOffsetTop = function(el) {
    var bodyRect = document.body.getBoundingClientRect(), elRect = el.getBoundingClientRect();
    return elRect.top - bodyRect.top;
  };
  self.getAdInView = function() {
    var scrollBoundary = self.playerOffsetTop + (self.playerHeight / 2), scrollTop = self.getScrollTop();
    return (window.innerHeight + scrollTop) > scrollBoundary && scrollTop < scrollBoundary;
  };
  // cross-browser event binding method
  self.setEventListener = function(el, ev, fn) {
    var eventMethod = window.addEventListener ? "addEventListener" : "attachEvent",
    eventName = window.addEventListener ? ev : "on" + ev;
    el[eventMethod](eventName, fn, false);
  };
  // get element margin top and bottom totat height
  self.getMarginHeight = function(el) {
    if (document.all) {
      return parseInt(el.currentStyle.marginTop, 10) + parseInt(el.currentStyle.marginBottom, 10);
    } else {
      return parseInt(document.defaultView.getComputedStyle(el, "").getPropertyValue("margin-top")) + parseInt(document.defaultView.getComputedStyle(el, "").getPropertyValue("margin-bottom"));
    }
  };
  // check if ad is in view, ad visible class when necessary (but only the first time it is in view)
  self.setAdDisplayState = function() {
    if (self.getAdInView()) {
      if (!new RegExp("(^| )jw-ad-visible( |$)", "gi").test(self.adEl.className)) {
        self.adEl.className += (self.adEl.className ? " " : "") + "jw-ad-visible";
        if(!false){
           self.adEl.style.maxHeight = self.adMediaContainerEl.offsetHeight + self.getMarginHeight(self.adMediaContainerEl) + "px";
           $(".jw-ad-media-container").append("<img id='thankyouId2' src =/Images/Pages/Results/EN-CA/Thank_you.jpg style=width:100%;height:100%;object-fit:cover;display:none; />"); 
        }
        else{
           self.adEl.style.maxHeight = "NaNpx";
        }
      }
      if(false && self.playerInstance.getState() === "idle" && !self.isClosed){
        setTimeout(function() {
          self.playerInstance.play();
        }, 0);
      }
      if (self.playerInstance.getState() === "paused" && !self.isClosed) {
        if(!($("#inviewvideoholder").hasClass("videoExpanded"))  && !false) { 
            $(".jw-ad").animate( 
               { }, 500, 
               () => { 
                $(".jw-ad").height("auto"); 
               $("#inviewvideoholder").addClass("videoExpanded");
            });
        } 
        setTimeout(function() {
          self.playerInstance.play();
        }, 0);
      }
    }
  };
  self.close = function() {
    self.isClosed = true;
   if(!false) {
       $(".jw-ad").animate( 
       { "padding-bottom": 0 }, 500, 
       () => { 
        $(".jw-ad").height("0"); 
       });
   }
   self.adEl.style.maxHeight = "0px";
   $("#inviewvideoholder").removeClass("inviewvideoholder");
   if ($(document.body).hasClass("edge")) {
     self.playerInstance.stop(); self.adMediaContainerEl.style.display = "none";
   } else {     self.playerInstance.remove();
    self.adMediaContainerEl.parentNode.removeChild(self.adMediaContainerEl);    }
  };
  self.init = function() {
    // player elements and utility vars
    if (self.jwhavejwplayerlib) {
      self.playerInstance = jwplayer("pRL6bZpgN2");
      self.adEl = document.querySelector(".jw-ad");
      self.adMediaContainerEl = document.querySelector(".jw-ad-media-container");
      self.playerHeight;
      self.playerOffsetTop = self.getElementOffsetTop(self.adEl);
      self.isScrollTimeout = false; // namespace for whether or not we are waiting for setTimeout() to finish
      // player setup
      if (self.jwhaveadditionaladtargets()) {
        if (self.jwhavedefaultadtag()) self.jwappenddefaultadtagwithadditional();
        if (self.jwhavescheduleadtag()) self.jwappendscheduleadtagwithadditional();
      }
      if (0) {
       self.playerInstance.setup({
           "file": "https://trader360videos.azureedge.net/national/blank1.mp4",
           "mediaid": "NSoGrA3w",
           "autostart": true,
           "mute": true,
           "withCredentials" : false,            "image": "",
           "advertising": {
               "tag": "",
               "client": "vast"
           }
       });
       self.playerInstance.resize(NaN,NaN);
      } else {
       self.playerInstance.setup({
           "file": "https://trader360videos.azureedge.net/national/blank1.mp4",
           "autostart": true,
           "mute": true,
           "mediaid": "NSoGrA3w"
       });
      }
    }
    self.playerInstance.on("adStarted", function() {
        if (!self.getAdInView()) {
           setTimeout(function() {
               self.playerInstance.pause();
           }, 0);
        }
        if(!false){
           $(".jw-ad").animate( 
               { "padding-bottom": "5px;" }, 500, 
               () => { 
                    $(".jw-ad").height("auto"); 
                   $("#inviewvideoholder").addClass("videoExpanded");
                });
         }
         $("#inviewvideoholder").addClass("inviewvideoholder");
         if(self.playerHeight === 0) {
             self.playerHeight = self.adMediaContainerEl.offsetHeight;
             self.playerOffsetTop = self.getElementOffsetTop(self.adEl);
         }
    });
    self.playerInstance.on("adTime", function (event) {            
       var remaining = Math.round(event.duration-event.position);  
       if(remaining == 0  && window.screen.width >= 768){           
            //self.playerInstance.seek(self.playerInstance.getDuration());            self.playerInstance.pause(); 
            $(".jw-text-alt").empty();                              
       }                                                           
    });                                                            
    self.playerInstance.on("ready", function() {
        self.isClosed = false;
        $("#inviewvideoholder").css("opacity", ""); 
        var closeBtn = "<span id=close>x</span>";
        $("#pRL6bZpgN2").append(closeBtn); 
        var closeElement = document.querySelector("#close");
        if (false) {
           $("#close").hide();
           self.playerInstance.resize(NaN,NaN);
        } else { 
           $("#close").css({ "position": "absolute", "top": "15px", "left": "10px", "color": "#FFF", "font-size": "2.5em", "z-index": "1", "cursor": "pointer" }); 
        }
       self.setEventListener(closeElement, "click", function () {
           self.close();
           $(".videoHolderHome").css({ "display": "none"}); 
       });
        // get player container height
        self.playerHeight = self.adMediaContainerEl.offsetHeight;
        // mute by default
        self.playerInstance.setMute(true);
        // handle ad display state on page load
        setTimeout(self.setAdDisplayState(), 1000);
        // attach scroll event listener to window
        self.setEventListener(window, "scroll", function() {
        // skip if we are waiting on a scroll update timeout to finish
        if (self.isScrollTimeout) return;
        // flag that a new timeout will begin
        self.isScrollTimeout = true;
        // otherwise, execute scroll event handler
        self.setAdDisplayState();
        // set new timeout
        setTimeout(function() {
          // reset timeout flag to false (no longer waiting)
          self.isScrollTimeout = false;
        }, 100);
      });
    });
    self.playerInstance.on("beforePlay", function () {
        if (false) {
           $("#inviewvideoholder").css("opacity", "");
        }
    });
    // handle when ad is complete or encounters error
    self.playerInstance.on("complete adComplete adError", function() {
      if (false  && !0) {
           $("#inviewvideoholder").hide();
      }
      if(!false &&  $("#inviewvideoholder").hasClass("inviewvideoholder") ){
         $("#thankyouId2").css({ "display": "block"}); 
         setTimeout(function() {
           $("#inviewvideoholder").css({ "margin-bottom": "10px"}); 
           $("#inviewvideoholder").removeClass("inviewvideoholder");
           $("#inviewvideoholder").removeClass("videoExpanded");
            $("#pRL6bZpgN2").detach();
         }, 500 /* should be the same duration as css transition */);
      }
    });
  };
};
$("#pRL6bZpgN2").ready(function() {
  p = new JwplayerWrapper2();
  p.init();
});</script></div>
